<review>Somewhat a mixed bag - but overall, if it was in my local area, I would NOT visit the place again. We ordered a couple of dishes - one was a vegetable stir fry and another one was eggplant. Both were asked to be made Thai Hot. The vegetable stir fry was bland - we were suggested to add the chili powder. Clearly, these people don't understand how to add chili during cooking and how that taste is totally different than just sprinkling chili powder. The eggplant dish on the other hand was as good as any that I have had elsewhere.

We also ordered Fried rice later and asked to hold the eggs. Unfortunately it came with eggs - the hostess apparently forgot to communicate to the cook. And this is where the main problem is. When we ask hostess to communicate our dietary preference - e.g. no egg/fish/oyster sauce, we expect that to be communicated. Otherwise, they are bringing to your table whatever they feel like. Breaking that trust is an absolute NO-NO for me - I never visit such places again.

Finally, to make the matters worst - even though the menu states that white/brown rice is included with the entree, we were charged extra for the brown rice. On pointing  that out, we were given a refund - but I shouldn't have to do that.< /review><pictures>None</pictures>< Response>

<Rate>1< /Rate>< text>
There were many things that went wrong with our meal. To start, we were the only people in the restaurant. We were kinda strapped for time because one person in our party had a business meeting in an hour, but it shouldve been plenty of time to eat and go.
When we got there the waitress was nowhere to be found and we waited about five minutes for her to appear and seat us. Then it took insanely long to get our drinks and order our food. At first it took ten minutes to get two small cups of starter salad, something that shouldve taken 30 seconds per bowl. After that there was a soup of the same size that took an additional ten minutes. Then we sat for another twenty minutes waiting for the dishes to arrive, but then only one came. each meal came one by one with like ten minutes in between. At this point we were really strapped for time and the two people who got their dishes 30 minutes after the first dish came had to eat super fast. I have to emphasize the fact that we were the only people in there, so it shouldve been so much faster.
And the service wasn't even the only thing that was sub par. I got pad see ew which is usually very saucy and flavorful, but this was barely sauced at all and only had like three pieces of tofu on it, and the noodles were really sticky. My boyfriend got pra-ram which he said tasted like canned food. Everyone's dish had veggies that had been steamed and then added after the fact to the plate, instead of cooking the veggies with the noodles etc. The veggies were floppy and wet. Even the Thai iced tea was weird.
The last thing was that this very weird guy was loitering around the restaurant making a point that he was only in there for the AC (it was 106 F) which is fine but when he started talking to us and asking questions it became weird and annoying.
Tldr; poor service, mediocre food, weird loitering men.</text>

We dropped into The Dish Thai Fusion Cuisine for some lunch while visiting a friend and chose this restaurant because it was the closest.

For a bit of backstory, I'd visited The Dish Thai Fusion Cuisine many years before at their other location and not really enjoyed my meal, but assumed it was either a chain or a new location so I didnt think much of trying it out again.

<username>Brian Batista< /username><time>1549570199971<//time><rating>1</rating>< text>
I have never written a review before but I figured it would be good to warn others of what I experienced with Jake Stewart.

I purchased my first vehicle ever when I was 24, a 2008 Honda Civic that I was financing from CarMax. Keyword being "financed" meaning it is illegal to drive the vehicle without proper 2-way coverage. I called State Farm and bought what I thought was the complete coverage at the time, putting all my faith in the insurance company that they were setting me up with what is the MINIMUM COVERAGE NEEDED FOR A FINANCED VEHICLE. 4 years go by and I had never missed a payment, and one day I am involved in a Hit and Run accident in Oakland that totaled my car and almost seriously injured myself and my passengers. When I call my insurance the next day, JAKE STEWART informed me that I, infact, only had liability coverage on the vehicle. HOW CAN THIS BE POSSIBLE IF THE VEHICLE IS STILL BEING FINANCED?? I told him that it must have been an error on their part because I have documentation showing that I told the writers of the policy that the vehicle was still being financed, yet they signed me up for the one way coverage anyways. I accept the blame that throughout the years I should have opened the policy and inspected my coverage, but I had simply put all my faith that they were doing the right thing for me and had my back which was not the case at all. Jake Stewart refused to help me. If I could have afforded to consult with a bad faith insurance attorney I would have done so immediately because something was not right with this situation. Jake Stewart left me with no vehicle and and remaining $10,000 balance on my car note that I was required to pay for a vehicle that was beyond repair. Moral of this story: Never trust insurance agents and always double check what you are paying for because when it hits the fan it won't be pretty. Here's to you, Jake.< /text>
<Pics>None</Pics>< resp>

There were also six documented mailings in that timeframe listing your coverages.  I am not sure what else we could have done to clarify how you were insured.  Every policyholder has the right to choose their own coverages and there is no way to "help" somebody after a claim if they wished they had chosen different coverages beforehand.  What remains surprising to me is why your lender didn\'t reach out to you if coverage was insufficient, as that is atypical behavior for them.
